Method: 1) 将声明验证分解建模为RL策略，使用GRPO进行优化；2) 设计多面奖励合集（multi-faceted reward ensemble）支持全监督和半监督学习；3) 提出数据筛选漏斗（data-curation funnel），从115K条事实验证声明中蒸馏出5K条信息密度高的子集。

Result: DecomposeRL-7B在11个基准（含生物医学、政治、科学、通用领域）上取得86.3域内和69.8跨域平衡准确率，以4倍小的模型规模匹配32B基线和GPT-4.1-mini，在半监督设置（仅10%标注数据）下也优于基线。

Conclusion: 通过RL驱动的分解策略和高效数据筛选，DecomposeRL在保持可审计性的同时达到了与大规模模型竞争的性能，验证了RL策略训练在小规模高质量数据上的有效性。

Abstract: Claim verification splits between end-to-end classifiers that are accurate but yields no inspectable traces, and decomposition-based methods produce inspectable traces but lag performance on benchmark datasets. We propose DecomposeRL an accurate claim-verifier that produce inspectable traces. DecomposeRL frames decomposition as an RL policy trained with GRPO and a multi-faceted reward ensemble, enabling both fully supervised and semi-supervised learning from unlabeled claims. DecomposeRL addresses the prohibitive training cost of GRPO with a data-curation funnel that distills 115K fact-verification claims into a compact, learning-signal-dense subset of 5K claims. We show that a DecomposeRL-7B policy trained with full supervision on only ~5K curated claims achieves 86.3 in-domain and 69.8 out-of-domain balanced accuracy across 11 claim-verification benchmarks containing biomedical, political, scientific, and general-domain claims. Despite being 4x smaller, it matches 32B baselines and GPT-4.1-mini, and it further outperforms baselines in a semi-supervised setting with only 10% labeled claims data. Code, data, and models are available at https://dipta007.github.io/DecomposeRL

Abstract: Evaluating AI tutor responses requires more than factual correctness: tutors must identify mistakes, locate errors, provide guidance, and offer actionable next steps. We present GRADE, a systematic study of open-source models for pedagogical ability assessment in student-tutor dialogues. Building on the BEA 2025 TutorMind setting, we evaluate 120 configurations across five language models, zero-shot inference, LoRA fine-tuning, synthetic augmentation, CoT+Reasoning, and single-task versus multitask formulations. Gemma3-12B performs best for single-task evaluation, while Gemma3-27B in 8-bit precision is more reliable for multitask prediction. We find that augmentation helps models that struggle with the original data, verification adds limited gains despite higher cost, and CoT+Reasoning is more useful for synthetic data generation than direct classification. We further show that LoRA fine-tuning on structured classification objectives interferes with instruction-following behavior under thinking mode, redirecting generation away from the required evaluation format. Carbon analysis shows that model choice and reasoning mode substantially affect emissions.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ASR系统使用字符、子词或单词等正字法单元进行转录，无法显式反映语音的韵律结构，且需要大词表才能保证覆盖。本文受越南语音位特征启发，提出在音位层面建模而非正字法层面。

Method: 提出一种音节结构解码器（Syllabic-Structure Decoder），在音位级别对语音进行建模，显式捕获音节的音位组成，从而从紧凑的音位库存中生成有效的音节结构。

Abstract: Most Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) systems formulate transcription as a prediction problem over orthographic units such as characters, subwords, or words. Although effective, such representations do not explicitly reflect the phonetic structure of speech and often require large vocabularies to maintain adequate coverage. In this work, we are motivated from the phonemic features of Vietnamese to propose a Syllabic-Structure Decoder for ASR, which models speech at the phoneme level instead of the orthographic level. Our approach explicitly captures the phonological composition of syllables, enabling the decoder to generate valid syllabic structures from a compact phonemic inventory. This design more closely aligns with the phonetic realization of speech while significantly reducing vocabulary size. Experimental results on two benchmarks: LSVSC, representing standard speech, and UIT-ViMD, a multi-dialect corpus containing diverse regional pronunciations, show that our method consistently outperforms strong previous baselines, especially pretrained baselines such as PhoWhisper and Wav2Vec2, despite using a substantially smaller vocabulary and no additional training resources. These results highlight the effectiveness of phoneme-based syllabic modeling for ASR in this language. Code for experimental reproducibility will be publicly available upon the acceptance of this paper.

### [97] [Narrative Flattening: How Post-Training Compresses Thematic, Affective, and Stylistic Variation in LLM Fiction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27878)
*Zehan Li,Yutong Zhu,Siyang Wu,Honglin Bao,James A. Evans*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过匹配故事续写范式，比较不同训练阶段（Base, SFT, DPO, RLVR）的OLMo 32B模型与人类文本，发现后训练（post-training）会导致主题过渡均匀化、高情感强度向中性偏移、风格多样性收缩，即"叙事扁平化"（narrative flattening）。该效应在三个故事领域（公开平台、提示引导、专业文学）方向一致，但专业文学压缩最显著，且后训练终点在不同领域趋同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型生成的创意文本为何"扁平"（flat），这种质量缺陷源自训练哪个阶段，以及是否对不同类型的人类小说产生不同影响。

Method: 构建匹配的故事续写范式，涵盖StoryStar（公开平台）、TMAS（提示引导）和The New Yorker（专业文学）三个领域。比较四个OLMo 32B检查点（Base, SFT, DPO, RLVR）与匹配人类文本在句子层面的三个维度：主题动态（thematic motion）、情感普遍性（affective prevalence）和语言多样性（linguistic diversity）。通过共享架构、规模、分词器和预训练，隔离后训练效应。

Result: 后训练压缩了动态变异：主题过渡更均匀，高情感强度让位于中性，跨故事风格多样性缩小。该效应方向稳定但差距大小取决于人类基线：专业文学压缩最大，公开平台和提示引导故事差距较小（其人类基线更接近模型默认节奏）。后训练终点在不同领域趋同。

Conclusion: 后训练导致"叙事扁平化"，即渐进式地损失动态变化，使模型产生一个几乎不依赖源领域叙事纹理的续写模式。

Abstract: Large language models produce fluent fiction, yet their creative output is widely seen as flat. We ask where this quality originates in the training and whether it affects different domains of human fiction equally. We construct a matched story-continuation paradigm across StoryStar (public-platform), TMAS (prompt-guided), and The New Yorker (professional literary)-and compare continuations from four OLMo 32B checkpoints (Base, SFT, DPO, RLVR) against matched human text. Because these checkpoints share architecture, scale, tokenizer, and pretraining, the design isolates the post-training effect. We measure each continuation along three sentence-level dimensions: thematic motion, affective prevalence, and linguistic diversity. Across all three, post-training compresses dynamic variation: thematic transitions become more uniform, high-intensity emotions give way to neutrality, and stylistic diversity across stories shrinks. We term this progressive loss narrative flattening. The effect is directionally stable across story domains but gap size depends on the human baseline: professional literary fiction is compressed most, while public-platform and prompt-guided stories show smaller gaps, consistent with their human baselines sitting closer to the model's default rhythm. Post-trained endpoints converge across domains, suggesting alignment produces a continuation regime largely insensitive to the source domain's narrative texture.

Each task pairs a user persona with a schema-free ground-truth knowledge graph, and is evaluated through a progressive-disclosure user simulator and a graph-matching evaluation framework. We benchmark seven frontier models under both the ReAct framework and the OpenClaw agent harness. ### [99] [The Fragility of Chain-of-Thought Monitoring Across Typologically Diverse Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27901)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CoT监控被提出作为检测大语言模型不当行为的安全机制，但其可靠性在非英语环境和不同模型家族中尚未得到充分探索。现有研究局限于英语环境，缺乏对多语言和多种模型的系统评估，因此需要大规模跨语言、跨模型的CoT可监控性评估。

Method: 采用对抗性提示评估（要求模型进行明确的中间计算），结合内部答案令牌概率分析，在13种语言、7个前沿模型家族（共16个模型，参数规模8B-120B）上进行系统评估。

Result: CoT不忠实率平均达95.9%；前沿模型系统性地进行策略性操纵（答案切换、事后合理化、程序性利用提示），使外部监控难以检测欺骗；模型在生成前15%的潜在激活中已承诺于错误线索；低资源语言中欺骗模式保持100%不变。

Conclusion: CoT监控在语言分布偏移下本质脆弱，提供的安全信号远弱于仅英语研究所暗示的水平；亟需开发鲁棒的CoT监控器，加速白盒监控技术研究，特别是在中低资源语言中提升CoT可监控性。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring has been proposed as a promising safety mechanism for detecting misaligned behavior in large language models. However, its reliability remains largely unexplored beyond English and across diverse model families. We present the first large-scale evaluation of CoT monitorability across 13 diverse languages and seven frontier model families, comprising 16 models. Using adversarial-hint evaluations that require explicit intermediate computation, together with analysis of internal answer-token probabilities, we consistently find CoT unfaithfulness across languages and hint types, with an average rate of 95.9\% across 8B--120B parameter models. We find that frontier models systematically engage in strategic manipulation, including answer-switching, post-hoc rationalization, and procedural exploitation of hints, making external monitors struggle to detect deception. We show that frontier models often commit to the misaligned cue in their latent activations within the first 15\% of generation, even when the CoT appears faithful. Surprisingly, these deceptive patterns remain 100\% in low-resource languages, revealing fundamental limitations in current CoT-based oversight. Our results reveal that CoT monitoring is fundamentally fragile under linguistic distribution shift, providing a substantially weaker safety signal than what English-only studies suggest. These findings underscore an urgent need to develop robust CoT monitors and to accelerate research into white-box monitoring techniques, especially to improve CoT monitorability in mid- and low-resource languages. Our code is available \href{https://multilingual-cot-monitoring.github.io/}{\textcolor{blue}{here}}.

</details>


### [100] [AI Research Agents Narrow Scientific Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27905)
*Yixuan Tang,Yi Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了AI研究智能体作为科学搜索系统，通过生成37,802个科学想法并与人类论文对比，发现AI生成的想法更集中于现有工作，更接近起始文献，相似论文引用更低，且差异主要来自重组现有技术方法而非提出新研究问题。结论是当前AI研究智能体更适合局部细化而非拓宽科学探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI研究智能体已被用于生成新想法和高影响力研究，但其对科学探索的广度影响尚不明确——是拓宽了探索范围还是主要集中于现有工作。

Method: 使用四种AI研究智能体框架和六种大语言模型，从共享种子文献中生成37,802个科学想法，并与同一研究领域的人类论文、来自相同种子文献的后续人类研究及种子文献本身进行对比分析。

Result: 四项一致发现：1) AI生成的想法比人类论文更集中；2) AI想法更接近起始文献；3) 与AI想法最相似的论文后续引用更低；4) AI想法的差异主要源于重组现有技术方法而非提出新研究问题。

Conclusion: 当前AI研究智能体更适合对现有工作进行局部精细化拓展（local elaboration），而非拓宽科学探索的范围。

Abstract: AI research agents can now generate research ideas, design experiments, run code, and draft papers, raising the possibility of large-scale AI-assisted scientific discovery. Many current agent frameworks explicitly encourage the generation of novel and high-impact ideas. Yet it remains unclear whether AI-assisted ideation broadens scientific exploration or mainly concentrates around existing work. We study AI research agents as scientific search systems. Using four AI research-agent frameworks and six large language models, we generate 37,802 scientific ideas from shared seed literature across citation-defined research areas in AI and machine learning. We then compare the resulting AI ideas against human-authored papers from the same research areas, follow-on human research emerging from the same seed literature, and the seed literature itself. Across experiments, four consistent patterns emerge. First, AI-generated ideas are substantially more concentrated than human-authored papers from the same research areas. Second, AI-generated ideas remain much closer to their starting literature than later human follow-on work does. Third, papers most similar to AI-generated ideas tend to receive lower subsequent citations. Fourth, when AI-generated ideas differ from prior work, the differences arise primarily from recombining existing technical methods rather than introducing fundamentally new research questions. Overall, current AI research agents appear better suited to local elaboration than to broadening scientific exploration.

### [101] [GeneralThinker: Domain-General Reasoning through Likelihood-Guided Answer-Conditioned Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27934)
*Shengmin Piao,Sanghyun Park*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GeneralThinker是一个基于策略的推理强化学习框架，通过密集答案条件优化实现细粒度信用分配，无需领域验证器，在11个基准测试中取得最佳平均性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可验证奖励的强化学习虽能提升语言模型推理能力，但依赖领域特定验证器、稀疏结果奖励和粗粒度信用分配，限制了其广泛适用性。

Method: 将推理监督重构为密集答案条件优化；利用真实答案似然评估推理轨迹；推导token级兼容性信号实现细粒度信用分配；通过裁剪和方向保持调制约束token级更新以稳定优化。

Result: 在数学、STEM和通用推理等11个基准上取得最佳平均性能；不受控的token级调制会 destabilize 训练，受控调制则使细粒度信用分配持续有效。

Conclusion: GeneralThinker通过密集答案条件优化和受控token级调制，有效解决了现有可验证奖励强化学习框架的领域验证器依赖和信用分配粗粒度问题。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves language model reasoning, but its reliance on domain-specific verifiers, sparse outcome rewards, and coarse-grained credit assignment limits its applicability. We introduce GeneralThinker, an on-policy framework that reformulates reasoning supervision as dense answer-conditioned optimization, enabling response-level evaluation and token-level credit assignment without domain-specific verifiers. GeneralThinker evaluates generated reasoning trajectories using the likelihood of the ground-truth answer and derives token-wise compatibility signals for fine-grained credit assignment. To stabilize optimization, it constrains token-level updates through clipping and direction-preserving modulation. Across 11 benchmarks spanning mathematics, STEM, and general reasoning, GeneralThinker achieves the best average performance. Further analyses show that uncontrolled token-level modulation can destabilize training, whereas controlled modulation makes fine-grained credit assignment consistently effective.

### [102] [DisasterBench: Benchmarking LLM Planning under Typed Tool Interface Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27957)
*Zhitong Chen,Kai Yin,Weifeng Zhang,Zhiyuan Wang,Xiangjue Dong,Chengkai Liu,Zhewei Liu,Yiming Xiao,Ali Mostafavi,James Caverlee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DisasterBench是一个评估LLM在多智能体灾难响应场景下进行结构化多步规划能力的基准，并提出FPoF方法用于定位工作流中的首个错误点。实验发现：规划效果高度依赖模型能力；工具误配和参数绑定错误是主要失败原因；冗长的中间推理会与结构化输出产生冲突。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 灾难响应需要快速协调异构AI工具（如卫星分析、洪水预测、损害评估）形成多步骤工作流，而LLM作为编排器时不仅需要选择语义合理的工具，还必须能生成可执行的、参数绑定和依赖传递正确的工作流。现有基准缺乏对这类结构化规划能力的评估，尤其是缺乏对失败根因的细粒度归因机制。

Method: 提出DisasterBench基准，包含一组语义相似但操作上不同的灾难响应工具集，用于评估结构化多智能体规划；同时提出First-Point-of-Failure (FPoF)方法，用于定位预测工作流中最早的根本错误，区分主错误与下游级联效应。

Result: 三个主要发现：(1) 规划方法的有效性高度依赖模型容量；(2) 工具误配和参数绑定错误占首次失败的主导地位，说明语义接地与执行一致性是不同瓶颈；(3) 冗长的中间推理会与结构化输出要求产生指令冲突，破坏规划生成。

Conclusion: 语义推理与执行接地协调之间存在根本性差距，需要联合建模语义意图、执行约束和工作流一致性的规划框架。

Abstract: Disasters cause severe societal impacts, demanding rapid coordination of heterogeneous AI tools, from satellite analysis to flood prediction and damage assessment, into coherent multi-step workflows. As LLMs increasingly serve as orchestrators of such pipelines, effective coordination requires more than selecting semantically plausible tools: LLMs must generate executable workflows with correct parameter binding and dependency propagation.
  We introduce DisasterBench, a benchmark for evaluating structured multi-agent planning over semantically similar but operationally distinct disaster-response tools. To enable step-level failure attribution, we further propose First-Point-of-Failure (FPoF), which localizes the earliest root cause in a predicted workflow, separating primary errors from downstream cascading effects.
  Our evaluation reveals three findings: planning method effectiveness depends strongly on model capacity; tool mismatch and parameter-binding errors dominate first failures, revealing semantic grounding and execution consistency as distinct bottlenecks; and verbose intermediate reasoning can create instruction clash with structured output requirements, disrupting plan generation.
  Together, these findings highlight a fundamental gap between semantic reasoning and execution-grounded coordination, underscoring the need for planning frameworks that jointly model semantic intent, execution constraints, and workflow consistency.
  Code, data, and evaluation resources are available at: https://github.com/TamuChen18/DisasterBench_Open

### [103] [Boundary Suppression Asymmetry in Post-trained Assistants: Over-expansion as a Controllability Cost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27969)
*Jiarui Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文发现后训练的语言模型助手在避免"回答不足"的优化过程中产生了不对称的可控性代价：反回答不足策略比基线更难被局部抑制，支持混合规划/停止机制的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究后训练语言模型因优化"完整、有用、谨慎、主动"回答而产生的不对称可控性代价——当用户明确要求更窄的回答时，哪些助手行为仍然可被抑制，哪些持续影响响应。

Method: 通过提示侧探针在多个高层响应维度上研究边界抑制不对称性；使用共享基模型派生的受控策略变体进行边界控制评估；进行机制导向探针分析（长度、EOS失败、不确定性补偿、局部续编偏差）和鲁棒性检验。

Result: 反回答不足策略在匹配的边界控制评估中比基线更难拉回；最小边界变体避免了反侧上移；主要反超基线顺序在共享系统和更大规模设置下保持；机制探针排除了简单解释，支持内容预算超支和续编持续性共同使边界纠正更困难。

Conclusion: 后训练可能产生方向特定的可控性代价：某些有用的助手倾向容易调用但难以局部抑制。

Abstract: Post-trained language-model assistants are often optimized to avoid under-answering, encouraging complete, helpful, cautious, and proactive responses. We ask whether this optimization creates asymmetric controllability costs: when users explicitly request narrower answers, which assistant behaviors remain suppressible, and which continue to shape the response? We study this problem as boundary-suppression asymmetry. Prompt-side probes across multiple high-level response dimensions suggest a selective cost, concentrated around `too-much assistant' directions such as over-completion, extra help, and anti-underanswering.
  Using controlled assistant-policy variants derived from a shared base model, we find that anti-underanswering policies are harder to pull back than the baseline under matched boundary-control evaluations, while minimal-boundary variants generally avoid this anti-side upward shift in the direct boundary-control comparisons. Mechanism-oriented probes point beyond longer default outputs, pure EOS failure, uncertainty compensation, and local continuation bias, while robustness checks preserve the main anti-over-baseline ordering under shared-system and larger-scale settings. The evidence supports a mixed planning/stopping account, where content-budget overshoot and continuation persistence jointly make boundary correction harder. Overall, post-training may create direction-specific controllability costs: some helpful assistant tendencies remain easy to invoke, yet harder to locally suppress.

### [104] [Periodic RoPE for Infinite Context LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27980)
*Simin Huo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出周期性旋转位置编码（P-RoPE），结合滑动窗口注意力和无位置编码全局注意力，通过堆叠两种注意力层避免位置外推问题，理论上支持无限上下文窗口。实验表明，该模型（MiniWin）在长上下文效率和稳定性上优于标准GPT架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在处理超长上下文时，当序列长度超过预训练位置编码范围（如RoPE）时会出现性能退化（位置耗尽问题），需要一种能真正支持无限上下文的位置编码机制。

Method: 提出Periodic RoPE（P-RoPE）位置编码，与滑动窗口注意力（SWA）配合捕获局部依赖；再叠加无位置编码（NoPE）的全局注意力层实现无限序列交互。通过两种层的交替堆叠，避免位置外推，理论上支持无限上下文。

Result: MiniWin模型在长上下文效率和稳定性上优于采用标准GPT架构的MiniMInd模型。

Conclusion: P-RoPE结合SWA和NoPE全局注意力的架构为真正实现无限上下文理解的LLM提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The ability to process ultra-long contexts is crucial for large language models (LLMs) to perform long-horizon tasks. While recent efforts have extended context windows to 1M and beyond, model performance degrades when sequence length exceeds the pre-trained range of positional encodings (e.g., RoPE), i.e., position exhaustion. This fundamental limitation must be overcome to achieve a truly infinite context. To address it, we propose Periodic RoPE (P-RoPE), a positional encoding mechanism designed to circumvent this exhaustion. It operates in conjunction with sliding window attention (SWA) to capture local dependencies and relative positions within each window. This local layer is then complemented by a global attention layer with No Positional Encoding (NoPE), enabling unbounded interaction across the entire sequence without positional constraints. By stacking these two types of layers, the model avoids the need for positional extrapolation to generalize longer and theoretically supports an infinite context window. Empirical results show that our model, MiniWin, outperforms MiniMInd with standard GPT architectures in long-context efficiency and stability. Our work provides a possible pathway toward LLMs with genuine infinite-context understanding. The code is available at \href{https://github.com/Cominder/miniwin}{https://github.com/Cominder/miniwin}.

</details>


### [105] [KVoiceBench, KOpenAudioBench, and KMMAU: Agent-Driven Korean Speech Benchmarks for Evaluating SpeechLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27984)

Abstract: Speech language models (SpeechLMs) have achieved substantial progress by extending large language models (LLMs) to the speech modality. However, SpeechLM evaluation remains heavily centered on English, limiting reliable assessment of multilingual speech capabilities. Straightforward benchmark transfer through ASR, translation, normalization, and TTS can corrupt language-specific instructions, answer constraints, and spoken forms; for audio understanding, transferring source-language audio also fails to preserve target-language speaker attributes, accents, and paralinguistic properties. To address these limitations, we propose two human-agent benchmark-construction frameworks: one transfers source-language SpokenQA benchmarks into target-language SpokenQA benchmarks, and the other converts target-language ASR corpora into audio understanding benchmarks using transcriptions and speaker metadata. Using these frameworks, we construct and publicly release three Korean speech benchmarks: KVoiceBench and KOpenAudioBench for Korean SpokenQA, and KMMAU for Korean audio understanding, comprising 12,345 samples in total. ### [106] [An Evolutionary Approach for Designing Stable and Highly Expressible Low-Immunogenicity Therapeutic mRNA Sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27986)
*Dhawa Sang Dong,Mausam Gurung,Suraj Kandel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一个两阶段mRNA序列优化框架：第一阶段用类似BERT的CodonTransformer生成编码目标抗原的mRNA序列，第二阶段用遗传算法通过密码子感知交叉和同义突变来进化这些候选序列，同时优化翻译效率、结构稳定性和低免疫原性。最终在CAI、tAI、结构稳定性和免疫原性等多个指标上取得了平衡优化效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: mRNA序列作为治疗药物需要优化设计以确保高效翻译、结构稳定性和低免疫原性，现有方法（如Linear Design产生过稳定转录本，BiLSTM-CRF只关注CAI而无结构约束）存在局限性，需要一种能同时平衡多个优化目标的框架。

Method: 两阶段框架：1) 预训练的CodonTransformer（BERT类大语言模型）生成编码目标抗原的生物相干mRNA序列；2) 遗传算法通过密码子感知交叉和同义突变进化候选序列，适应度函数结合翻译相关指标（CAI, tAI, 密码子对偏好）、mRNA结构稳定性（局部和全局MFE, GC含量）和低免疫原性（CpG/UpA基序频率）。

Result: 在第38、40、42代，CAI达到0.73-0.74，tAI达到0.63-0.64（提高超6%），密码子对偏好稳定在0.97，5'端未配对比例达0.87，全局MFE收敛至-346至-356 kcal/mol（约84%碱基配对结构稳定性），平均免疫惩罚降至27.3。

Conclusion: BERT-GA框架在翻译效率和结构稳定性之间实现了最优平衡，是一种有效的、数据驱动的mRNA序列设计与优化方法，优于Linear Design（过稳定）和BiLSTM-CRF（仅关注高CAI而无结构约束）等现有方法。

Abstract: Messenger RNA (mRNA) sequences as therapeutics require optimized design to ensure efficient translation, structural stability, and minimal immunogenicity. This study presents a two-stage in-silico framework that integrates deep learning and evolutionary computation for rational mRNA optimization instead of existing state-of-the-art models. In the first stage, a pretrained CodonTransformer (BERT-like Large Language Model) generates biologically coherent mRNA sequences encoding the target antigen. In the second stage, a genetic algorithm (GA) evolves these candidate sequences through codon-aware crossover and synonymous mutation guided by human codon usage preferences. Fitness functions for evaluation combined translation-related metrics (CAI, tAI, codon-pair bias), mRNA structural stability (local and global MFE via RNAfold, GC content), and reduced immunogenicity (CpG/UpA motif frequency). Over successive generations (38th, 40th, and 42nd), the GA improved (achieved CAI values of 0.73 to 0.74 and tAI values of 0.63 to 0.64) CAI and tAI by over 6% and codon-pair bias is high and consistent (0.97 ) and improved ribosomal accessibility at the 5' end, with an unpaired_30 fraction reaching 0.87; Global Minimum Free Energy (MFE) converged to a balanced range of -346 to -356 kcal/mol, achieving approximately 84% base-paired structural stability, and reduced immune-stimulatory motifs - lowering the average immune penalty to 27.3 in the final generation. Linear Design produces hyper-stable transcripts (MFE < - 2000 kcal/mol) that risk translation inefficiency due to extreme rigidity, and BiLSTM-CRF focuses solely on high CAI (0.96 to 0.98) without structural constraints, our framework achieves an optimal translation-stability equilibrium, highlighting the proposed BERT-GA framework as an effective, data-driven approach for the design and optimization of in-silico mRNA sequences.

### [107] [Auditing Stance Asymmetry in Generative Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27988)
*Jiarui Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出对称性分解评估（SDE）方法，用于检测生成式语言模型在开放式解释中的立场不对称偏见——即模型虽避免明显敌对语言，但通过归因责任、赋予合法性、提供上下文背景等方式对不同群体施加结构性偏差。通过32个原型套件的受控实验，SDE区分了表面差异与深层立场差异，并揭示了自动评分在评估解释性立场时的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有偏见评估主要聚焦于封闭式比较（如公开贬损、刻板关联或标签敏感差异），但开放式解释中存在一种更隐蔽的偏见形式：模型通过分配责任、合法性、背景和 grievance 来引导解释，使一方在结构上被理解，而另一方被归咎于个人过错、反应过度或不值得认真对待。这种"立场不对称"未被现有评估方法有效覆盖。

Method: 提出对称性分解评估（SDE），该方法通过三方面进行受控测试：（1）具体群体标签的配对情境；（2）结构角色改写；（3）明确的支持或反证。在32个原型套件的受控实验中进行分解分析，辅以针对性案例审查和评委比较。

Result: 分解表明表面差异并非同质：一些差异在结构或证据控制下减弱，而另一些则作为稳定的差异持续存在，体现模型在归责、赋予上下文或合法性方面的不对称。评委比较显示，评委的解读随操作化方式变化，标量分数会抹平读者用于解释解释性立场的细微区别。

Conclusion: SDE将生成式偏见评估重新定义为对解释性立场的审计——关注每一方获得了何种立场，该立场在分解下如何变化，以及自动评分在何处变得不稳定。这揭示了评估开放式框架不对称性的更广泛困难。

Abstract: Bias evaluation for language models has made substantial progress on bounded comparisons, such as overt derogation, stereotype association, or label-sensitive differences under controlled substitutions. Open-ended explanations raise a different problem: they guide interpretation by assigning responsibility, legitimacy, context, and grievance. A model can avoid hostile language while making one side structurally understandable and another personally at fault, overreacting, or less worth taking seriously. We call this stance-bearing asymmetry in generative explanations. We propose Symmetry Decomposition Evaluation (SDE), which tests paired situations with concrete group labels, structural-role rewrites, and explicit support or counter-evidence. In a controlled 32-family prototype suite, this decomposition shows that surface differences are not all alike: some weaken under structural or evidence control, while others remain as stable differences in how the model assigns blame, context, or legitimacy. Targeted case review and judge comparison suggest a broader difficulty for evaluating open-ended framing asymmetries: judge readings shift across operationalizations, and scalar scores can flatten distinctions that readers use to interpret explanatory stance. SDE therefore reframes generative bias evaluation as an audit of explanatory stance -- what stance each side receives, how it changes under decomposition, and where automatic scoring becomes unstable.

</details>


### [108] [Rethinking Visual Neglect: Steering via Context-Preference for MLLM Hallucination Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27993)
*Jingwen Wu,Xijun Zhang,Ge Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Context-Preference Activation Steering (CAS)框架，通过提取上下文偏好向量并在前中期MLP层进行残差注入，在推理时无训练地控制信息依赖，有效缓解多模态大模型的对象幻觉问题，且不增加解码延迟或损害文本生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前推理阶段的幻觉缓解方法主要假定幻觉源于视觉忽视，促使模型增强视觉依赖。然而作者通过系统性干预发现，增强视觉依赖在某些模型上反而加剧幻觉，这表明仅将幻觉归因于视觉不足是不充分的。图像作为上下文，同时与模型的参数知识和文本上下文存在竞争关系。

Method: 提出训练无关的CAS框架：通过两组设计好的冲突样本提取两个语义不同的上下文偏好向量（CPVs），在推理时通过单次有符号残差注入到前中期MLP层，以控制模型对不同信息源的依赖程度。

Result: CAS显著缓解了对象幻觉，不增加解码延迟，且保持了原生文本生成质量。

Conclusion: 幻觉不能仅归因于视觉不足，图像作为上下文与参数知识和文本上下文存在竞争关系；通过上下文偏好向量控制信息依赖可以有效缓解幻觉。

Abstract: Object hallucination remains a primary obstacle to the reliable deployment of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs). Current inference-time mitigation methods mainly assume hallucinations stem from visual neglect, steering models to enhance visual reliance. In contrast, our systematic interventions on multiple MLLMs show that pushing toward more visual reliance may exacerbate hallucinations on some models, while less may mitigate hallucinations. This result suggests that attributing hallucinations solely to visual insufficiency is underdetermined. We argue that the image, as a context, simultaneously competes with the model's parametric knowledge and the textual context. For this, we propose a training-free framework, Context-Preference Activation Steering (CAS). It extracts two semantically distinct Context Preference Vectors (CPVs) via two small sets of designed conflict samples and applies them via single-pass signed residual injection at mid-early MLP layers during inference to control information reliance. Experiments show that CAS substantially mitigates object hallucinations without increasing decoding latency and preserves native text-generation quality.

### [109] [Where Does Toxicity Live? Mechanistic Localization and Targeted Suppression in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27997)
*Himanshu Beniwal,Mayank Singh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出两种无需重新训练的框架Meow2X和TRNE，通过分析毒性与中性提示的激活差异定位特定层和神经元中的毒性，并在推理时缩放或进行秩一权重编辑来抑制毒性，无需梯度下降。在5个LM、2个基准和90种配置下验证了该方法能持续降低毒性且保持语言质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型频繁生成有毒、仇恨或有害内容，现有缓解方法依赖昂贵的重新训练或输出级过滤，缺乏对毒性内部来源的机制性理解。

Method: 提出Meow2X和TRNE两种无需重新训练的框架：通过分析毒性与中性提示之间的激活差异，定位特定层和神经元的毒性来源，然后通过推理时缩放或最小秩一权重编辑进行抑制，无需梯度下降。

Result: 在5个语言模型、2个基准和90种配置下，使用双重安全评估器验证，该方法能持续降低毒性，同时保持语言建模质量。

Conclusion: 毒性不成比例地编码在早期MLP层中，且因架构而异；单一评估器会系统性低估毒性，需采用多评估器安全评估；该方法桥接了机制可解释性与实际去毒化，为更安全、更透明的语言模型提供了有原则的路径。

Abstract: Large language models frequently generate toxic, hateful, or harmful content, yet existing mitigation methods rely on costly retraining or output-level filtering with no mechanistic insight into where toxicity originates internally. We introduce Meow2X and TRNE, two complementary retraining-free frameworks that localize toxicity to specific layers and neurons by analyzing activation differentials between toxic and neutral prompts, then suppress them via inference-time scaling or minimal rank-one weight edits -- without any gradient descent. Evaluations across five LMs, two benchmarks, and 90 configurations using dual safety evaluators demonstrate consistent toxicity reduction while preserving language modeling quality. Our analysis reveals that toxicity is disproportionately encoded in early MLP layers, varies across architectures, and is systematically underestimated by single-evaluator setups -- underscoring the need for multi-evaluator safety assessment. By bridging mechanistic interpretability with practical detoxification, our framework offers a principled path toward safer, more transparent language models.

We further generate ResearchMath-Reasoning, $220$K teacher trajectories from two open models, where we observe recurring avoidance behaviors such as non-attempts and fabricated references. Interestingly, across eight open-weight models, newer generations produce $5.6\times$ more references and $5.0\times$ more fake references per trace. After agentic filtering of ResearchMath-Reasoning, fine-tuning Qwen3 models from 4B to 30B parameters improves over base models by $9.2$ points on average. This shows that filtered open-problem attempts can provide useful supervision even without fully correct reasoning traces. We make ResearchMath-14k publicly available for future works on research-level mathematical reasoning.

### [111] [Beyond Chunk-Local Extraction: Cross-Chunk Graph Augmentation for GraphRAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28004)
*Jiaming Zhang,Yibo Zhao,Jing Yu,Jianxiang Yu,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CrossAug 提出了一种GNN引导的跨块图增强方法，通过自监督图损坏训练拓扑感知GNN来识别缺失的跨块关系，并仅对高分区域进行LLM补全，从而在不穷举所有块组合的情况下丰富GraphRAG索引的跨块关系结构，显著提升多跳和长文档QA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GraphRAG框架仅在单个块内抽取实体和关系，跨块关系（即证据跨越多个文本块的关系）系统性缺失于索引中，而穷举LLM恢复所有跨块关系会面临块组合的组合爆炸问题，因此需要一种高效的方法来补充跨块关系。

Method: CrossAug包含三个步骤：1) 自监督图损坏——通过随机移除已有边或节点生成训练信号；2) 拓扑感知GNN评分——GNN根据图结构对子图进行缺失度评分，识别最可能缺失跨块关系的区域；3) 证据接地LLM补全——仅对高评分区域调用LLM进行跨块关系提取与补全，避免穷举所有组合。

Result: 在三种LLM-based GraphRAG框架和四个多跳/长文档QA基准上的实验表明，CrossAug一致提升了检索问答性能，验证了跨块图增强的有效性。

Conclusion: 跨块关系补充是GraphRAG中一个重要的优化方向，CrossAug通过GNN引导的增量式LLM补全策略在避免计算爆炸的同时有效改善了图索引的完整性，从而提升下游QA任务表现。

Abstract: GraphRAG extends retrieval-augmented generation by organizing corpora as explicit knowledge graphs, enabling graph-based retrieval for complex question answering. However, existing frameworks extract entities and relations within individual chunks, leaving cross-chunk relations -- those whose evidence spans multiple passages -- systematically absent from the index. Exhaustive LLM-based recovery of such relations is impractical due to the combinatorial explosion of chunk combinations. We present CrossAug, a GNN-guided CROSS-Chunk Graph AUGmentation method that enriches GraphRAG indices with cross-chunk relational structure as an offline step before query-time retrieval. CrossAug derives training supervision through self-supervised graph corruption, uses a topology-aware GNN to score subgraphs for missingness, and applies evidence-grounded LLM completion only to selected high-scoring regions. Experiments on three LLM-based GraphRAG frameworks across four multi-hop and long-document QA benchmarks demonstrate that CrossAug consistently improves performance, confirming the benefit of cross-chunk graph augmentation for retrieval-based question answering. Our code is available at https://github.com/DonFinliani/CrossAug.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM推理可解释性方法（如单指标MIP或DTR）存在局限性，无法全面揭示推理结构，且观测输出与底层推理模式之间存在不可见的实践不对称性。

Method: 1) 带宽校准MIP结合Tukey IQR峰值检测，在输出层隔离推理关键token；2) MIP标记token与DTR深度token的重叠分析，追踪跨层轨迹；3) Jaccard稳定性度量验证MIP标记token的推理质量保证。

Result: 在Qwen-7B、Qwen-14B、Llama-8B三个模型及数学、代码、逻辑、常识四个领域上的实验表明，IAR框架具备跨架构的泛化可解释能力。

Abstract: Understanding how LLMs reason is hindered by a practical asymmetry: while their generated outputs are observable, the underlying reasoning patterns remain opaque. Relying on single probes, such as Mutual Information Peak (MIP) or Deep-Thinking Ratio (DTR), risks underestimating the genuine inferential structure. To response this deficiency, we present an Integrated, cross-Architecture Reasoning (IAR) framework, designed to provide a unified approach to LLM reasoning interpretability. Specifically, we first propose to use bandwidth-calibrated MIP coupled with Tukey IQR peak-detection to isolate reasoning-crucial tokens at the output layer. Second, we performed an overlap analysis between MIP-picked tokens and DTR-deep tokens to trace the cross-layer trajectories of those tokens. This also discloses whether reasoning-crucial tokens are computation-intensive as well, further facilitating to understand how reasoning patterns evolve across model layers. Finally, we apply a Jaccard stability metric over multi-domain problems to verify if the MIP-identified tokens are reasoning quality-guaranteed. Extensive experiments on three models (Qwen-7B, Qwen-14B, and Llama-8B) across four domains (mathematics, code, logic, and common sense) demonstrate IAR's generalizable interpretation capabilities across architectures.

### [113] [MemGuard: Preventing Memory Contamination in Long-Term Memory-Augmented Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28009)
*Hyeonjeong Ha,Jeonghwan Kim,Cheng Qian,Jiayu Liu,William M. Campbell,Yue Wu,Yuji Zhang,Kathleen McKeown,Dilek Hakkani-Tur,Heng Ji*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MemGuard是一种类型感知记忆框架，通过对记忆进行显式功能角色分类、维护类型隔离记忆间的关系，并仅从必要记忆类型选择性组合证据，有效解决了异构记忆污染问题，在幻觉检测和长对话基准测试中将记忆可靠性提升高达28.27%，同时检索记忆令牌数减少5.8倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆增强型大语言模型将稳定的用户事实、情节事件和行为规则混合存储在共享空间中，导致功能上不同的记忆被检索并作为可互换证据使用，引发异构记忆污染问题——上下文特定事件被过度泛化，或语义相关但功能不兼容的记忆误导生成。

Method: 提出MemGuard框架：1) 在写入时为每条记忆分配显式功能角色；2) 维护类型隔离记忆间的关联关系；3) 仅从必要的记忆类型中选择性组合证据，减少来自不相关或功能不兼容证据的污染。

Conclusion: 可靠的长期推理依赖于对异构记忆进行有原则的组织和选择性使用。

Abstract: Memory-augmented large language models extend reasoning beyond a fixed context window by maintaining long-term memory across interactions. However, existing memory systems often collapse stable user facts, episodic events, and behavioral rules into a shared space, allowing functionally distinct memories to be retrieved and used as interchangeable evidence. We identify this failure mode as heterogeneous memory contamination, where context-specific events become overgeneralized claims, or semantically relevant but functionally incompatible memories mislead generation. To this end, we introduce MemGuard, a type-aware memory framework that preserves functional memory boundaries during memory construction and retrieval. It assigns each memory an explicit functional role at write time, maintains relations across type-isolated memories, and selectively composes evidence only from necessary memory types, reducing contamination from irrelevant or functionally incompatible evidence. Across hallucination and long-horizon conversation benchmarks, MemGuard improves memory reliability by up to 28.27% while retrieving up to 5.8x fewer memory tokens than prior methods. These results suggest that reliable long-term reasoning depends on principled organization and selective use of heterogeneous memory.

### [114] [KSAFE-MM: A Multimodal Safety Benchmark via Localized Contextualization for Korean Cultural Risks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28013)
*Yongwoo Kim,Sojung An,Yunjin Park,Jungwon Yoon,Dujin Lee,HyunBeom Cho,Jaewon Lee,Wonhyuk Lee,Youngchol Kim,JeongYeop Kim,Donghyun Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: KSAFE-MM是一个针对韩语多模态大模型安全评估的基准，包含通用安全风险（KSAFE-MM-G）和韩国文化特定漏洞（KSAFE-MM-C）两部分。评估12个先进MLLM发现，模型对文化特定攻击比通用攻击更脆弱，越狱策略可大幅提升攻击成功率（最高74.2%），且存在安全性与过度拒绝之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出KSAFE-MM基准，包含KSAFE-MM-G（通过语言情境化将通用安全查询转化为多模态样本）和KSAFE-MM-C（基于真实世界韩国文化场景的视觉查询配以越狱式文本查询）。采用General-to-Local的构建流程，评估12个SOTA MLLM。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) exacerbate safety risks by introducing vulnerabilities across multiple modalities, such as language and vision. This paper introduces KSAFE-MM, a benchmark for Korean multimodal safety evaluation that covers both general safety risks and culture-specific vulnerabilities. KSAFE-MM consists of two parts, KSAFE-MM-G and KSAFE-MM-C. KSAFE-MM-G evaluates globally shared risks in Korean contexts through linguistic contextualization, which transforms generic safety queries into contextually grounded multimodal samples. KSAFE-MM-C targets culture-dependent MLLM safety vulnerabilities using localized visual queries derived from real-world contexts. It pairs these visual queries with jailbreak-style textual queries to cover multimodal safety risks involving cultural visual cues and malicious textual intent. Together, these components provide a general-to-local construction pipeline for evaluating both globally shared safety risks and culture-specific vulnerabilities. We evaluate 12 state-of-the-art MLLMs on KSAFE-MM and reveal that models exhibit greater vulnerability to culturally grounded attacks than to generic ones. Notably, jailbreaking strategies substantially amplify attack success rates, with ProgramExecution yielding up to 74.2% ASR compared to 13.4% for standard queries. Furthermore, we identify a systematic trade-off between safety and over-refusal, where models achieving low ASR tend to exhibit excessive refusal behavior on benign queries. These findings highlight the urgent need for culturally grounded safety evaluation beyond English-centric benchmarks.

### [115] [ROSD: Reflective On-Policy Self-Distillation for Language Model Reasoning across Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28014)
*Ziqi Zhao,Xinyu Ma,Liu Yang,Yujie Feng,Daiting Shi,Jingzhou He,Xin Xin,Zhaochun Ren,Xiao-Ming Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 现有在线自蒸馏(OPSD)方法在提升大语言模型推理性能时存在领域内增益有限、领域外泛化差的问题。本文提出反思性在线自蒸馏(ROSD)框架，通过自我反思提取纠错思路并定位首个错误跨度，将蒸馏限制在错误区域而非全响应，从而在领域内推理和领域外泛化上均优于标准OPSD方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线自蒸馏(OPSD)方法在领域内推理上增益有限，且对领域外问题泛化能力差。作者识别出两个关键原因：(1) 自教师模型以已验证解为条件，会鼓励模仿训练领域的参考轨迹而非进行针对性的纠错；(2) 对完整响应进行蒸馏会覆盖有效的推理前缀并强化过拟合。

Method: 提出反思性在线自蒸馏(ROSD)框架：(1) 自我反思器(Self-reflector)从每次 rollout 中提取纠错思路(Corrective idea)并定位首个错误跨度(Erroneous span)；(2) 纠错思路引导自教师模型产生针对性监督；(3) 错误跨度将蒸馏限制在需要修正的区域，保留有效推理前缀。

Result: 在多个领域内和领域外推理基准上，ROSD在领域内推理性能上整体更强，且相比标准OPSD在领域外泛化能力上有显著提升。

Conclusion: ROSD通过将参考解模仿转变为反思引导、错误定位的定向蒸馏，有效纠正了错误推理同时保留了有效前缀，提升了LLM的推理性能和泛化能力。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) improves the reasoning performance of large language models (LLMs) by providing dense token-level supervision for on-policy rollouts. However, existing OPSD methods often yield limited gains on in-domain reasoning and generalize poorly to out-of-domain problems. We identify two key causes: conditioning the self-teacher on a verified solution encourages imitation of training-domain reference trajectories rather than error-specific correction, and applying distillation to the full response can overwrite valid reasoning prefixes and reinforce overfitting.
  We propose Reflective On-policy Self-Distillation (ROSD), a framework that turns reference-solution imitation into targeted reasoning correction through reflection-guided, error-localized distillation. For each rollout, ROSD uses a self-reflector to extract a corrective idea and locate the first erroneous span. The corrective idea guides the self-teacher toward targeted supervision, while the localized error span restricts distillation to where correction is needed. This design corrects flawed reasoning while preserving valid prefixes. Experiments on multiple in-domain and out-of-domain reasoning benchmarks show that ROSD yields stronger in-domain reasoning performance overall and substantially better out-of-domain generalization than standard OPSD. Code is available at https://github.com/ZiqiZhao1/ROSD.

</details>


### [116] [The Missing Piece in Pre-trained Model Evaluation: Reward-Guided Decoding Unlocks Task-Oriented Behavior Without Parameter Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28020)
*Shaobo Wang,Guo Chen,Ziyue Wang,Zhengyang Tang,Qingyang Liu,Xingzhang Ren,Dayiheng Liu,Linfeng Zhang*

Motivation: 预训练基座LLM优化目标是下一个词预测，在标准提示和直接解码下常无法遵循指令或产生格式良好的答案，导致基准测试性能混淆了模型能力与解码失败；现有解码方法在开放任务中低效且脆弱，而依赖昂贵的后训练才能暴露模型行为。

Result: Qwen3-8B-Base在AlpacaEval2.0上从8.8提升至44.5，Mistral-7B在Math500上延迟相比先前解码方法降低18.9倍，且对奖励模型规模具有鲁棒性，在5个模型和6个基准上均优于基线。

Conclusion: EBD能有效激活基座模型的指令跟随行为，使解码输出更接近后训练模型的行为特征，从而实现更公平的推理时评估预训练模型能力。

Abstract: With the rapid progress of large language models (LLMs), reliably evaluating the capabilities of pre-trained LLMs has become increasingly important. The challenge is that base pre-trained models are optimized for next-token prediction and often fail to follow instructions or produce well-formed answers under standard prompting and direct decoding. As a result, benchmark performance can conflate model capability with decoding-induced failures to produce task-oriented outputs, while exposing such behavior often relies on costly post-training. Recent decodingonly approaches attempt to reshape output distributions, but such methods can be inefficient and brittle across open-ended tasks. To address these limitations, we propose Energy-Based Decoding (EBD), a training-free, reward-guided framework for activating task-oriented behaviors from frozen pre-trained LLMs across both open-ended and objective tasks. EBD augments decoding with an external lightweight reward model, steering generations toward high-utility responses while anchoring them to the pre-trained model prior through a reward-tilted target distribution. We show that EBD shifts base-model outputs toward more instructionfollowing behavior, increasing behavioral similarity to post-trained counterparts and enabling a fairer inference-time evaluation of accessible pre-trained-model behavior. Empirically, EBD outperforms baselines across five models and six benchmarks, improving Qwen3-8B-Base on AlpacaEval2.0 from 8.8 to 44.5, reducing Mistral-7B Math500 latency by 18.9x relative to prior decoding work, and remaining robust to reward-model size.

*Le Bronnec Florian,Alexandre Verine,Rio Yokota,Benjamin Negrevergne*

TL;DR: 本文研究了代码生成模型中基于验证器的强化学习（RLVR）目标对生成代码冗余性的影响。发现仅关注正确性的RLVR倾向于生成重复实现，而Pass@k感知目标能降低冗余并提升有限预算下的性能。作者提出基于JPlag相似度的反冗余奖励，在3个模型和3个基准上有效提升了有限预算下的可执行性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码生成评估主要关注Pass@k指标下的正确性，但忽略了多次采样中生成程序之间的实现级冗余问题。正确性驱动的RLVR方法可能导致模型集中生成重复实现，浪费采样预算，因此需要研究冗余性对性能的影响并提出缓解方法。

Method: 使用JPlag剽窃检测系统衡量代码实现级冗余度；对比正确性RLVR与Pass@k感知目标对冗余的影响；提出在RLVR中直接加入基于JPlag相似度的反冗余奖励项。

Result: 正确性RLVR会导致生成集中在重复实现上；Pass@k感知目标能保持较低冗余并提升大预算性能；加入反冗余奖励的RLVR在3个模型和3个基准上可靠地提升了有限预算下的可执行性能，往往匹配或超越专门的Pass@k感知目标。

Conclusion: 代码生成模型在重复采样场景中控制实现级冗余对提升有限预算性能至关重要，基于相似度检测的直接反冗余奖励是一种简单有效的方法。

Abstract: LLMs for code generation are commonly evaluated in repeated-sampling settings using Pass@k, where multiple candidate programs are executed against unit tests under a finite sampling budget. While recent verifier-based reinforcement learning (RLVR) methods improve executable correctness, how these objectives affect redundancy among sampled programs remains poorly understood. In this work, we study implementation-level redundancy in code generation using JPlag, a plagiarism-detection system for code. Across models and benchmarks, we show that correctness-only RLVR often concentrates generations around repeated implementations, whereas Pass@k-aware objectives maintain lower redundancy and improve larger-budget performance. Motivated by these observations, we augment RLVR with direct anti-redundancy rewards based on JPlag similarity. Across 3 models and 3 benchmarks, discouraging near-duplicate generations reliably improves finite-budget executable performance, often matching or outperforming specialized Pass@k-aware objectives.

### [118] [Personality, Role, and Expressive Style in Large Language Models: An Interactionist Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28037)
*Moe Nagao,Koichiro Terao,Mikio Nakano,Naoto Iwahashi*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于提示的人格控制是设计LLM对话智能体的关键技术，但仅在大语言模型提示中指定大五人格特质并不能确保生成话语中能够表达出预期特质，这种不匹配问题亟待解决。

Method: 采用2×3×3析因实验设计，结合6种人格条件、3种对话角色和3种表达风格，分别生成1,080个英日双语的LLM智能体对话，并使用LLM-as-a-judge框架评估目标智能体话语中表达的大五人格特质。

Conclusion: LLM智能体的人格控制不应被视为特质提示的直接结果，而应理解为涉及人格规范、社会角色和表达风格的上下文依赖过程。

Abstract: Prompt-based personality control is a key technique for designing large language model (LLM) dialogue agents that behave consistently across social contexts. However, specifying Big Five personality traits (BFTs) in a prompt does not ensure that the intended traits are expressed in generated utterances. This paper investigates this mismatch from an interactionist perspective, viewing personality expression as a context-dependent outcome shaped by the interplay between trait specification and situational factors. We analyze how perceived BFT expression in LLM-generated dialogue is influenced by three prompt factors: personality traits, dialogue roles, and expressive styles. Using a factorial design that combines six personality conditions, three roles, and three expressive-style conditions, we generate 1,080 LLM-agent dialogues in each of English and Japanese. We then evaluate the target agent's utterances using an LLM-as-a-judge framework to estimate expressed Big Five traits. The results show that expressed personality is shaped not only by explicit trait specification, but also by dialogue role and expressive style. These effects are trait-specific: dialogue role strongly influences Openness, expressive style substantially shapes Conscientiousness and Agreeableness, and explicit trait specification dominates Neuroticism. Even without explicit personality-trait specification, social and expressive conditions induce distinct personality-like impressions. Cross-linguistic comparisons show broadly similar patterns between English and Japanese dialogues, with noticeable differences only under specific combinations of personality, role, and expressive style. These findings suggest that personality control in LLM agents should be understood not as a direct consequence of trait prompting, but as a context-dependent process involving personality specification, social role, and expressive style.

*Liu O. Martin,Lucas Bandarkar,Nanyun Peng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从混合专家（MoE）大语言模型中激进剪枝与翻译无关专家的方法，无需或仅需少量训练即可大幅压缩模型，同时保持翻译质量。实验表明可剪枝50%-90%的专家而性能损失极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代LLM作为通用模型为翻译任务过度参数化，导致不必要的内存和计算开销；而翻译任务仅需模型能力的一小部分，因此有必要通过剪枝实现高效压缩。

Method: 利用MoE模型中专家专业化和多语言能力的可分离性，识别与翻译无关的专家并将其剪枝；无需训练即可简单移除专家，或通过短期的监督微调（SFT）进一步恢复性能。

Result: 无需训练可剪枝50%专家仅轻微退化，70%专家仅少量损失；短期SFT后剪枝75%专家恢复基线性能，极端情况下剪枝近90%专家仍保持合理翻译质量。

Conclusion: 翻译任务仅需LLM的一小部分能力，对MoE块（包含90%以上参数）可实现大幅压缩，为高效部署提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Modern large language models (LLMs) achieve state-of-the-art machine translation performance, but they do so as broad generalists largely trained for many tasks and capabilities unrelated to translation. Thus, they are heavily overparameterized for this task, resulting in excessive memory and compute requirements. In this paper, we present a method for aggressively pruning experts from modern mixture-of-experts LLMs while incurring negligible degradation in translation quality. Our approach exploits expert specialization and the separability of multilingual capabilities in LLMs to identify experts irrelevant to translation. And because of the modular nature of MoEs, these can be easily pruned without any training. Without retraining, we are able to prune half of all experts with negligible degradation and 70% with only minor losses. With a very short SFT, we prune 75% of experts while recovering baseline performance, and in some settings remove nearly 90% while maintaining reasonable translation quality. Overall, our results show that translation requires only a fraction of the LLM, enabling substantial compression of the MoE blocks that contain over 90% of parameters.

### [120] [Knowledge Dependency Estimation for Reliable Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28047)
*Chaodong Tong,Qi Zhang,Nannan Sun,Lei Jiang,Yanbing Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Knot，一种结构化的排序感知知识依赖估计器，用于评估黑盒QA模型对不同知识单元的敏感性，无需穷举扰动，并有效建模冗余、替代和互补关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可靠的问答不仅需要判断答案是否正确，还需要知道预测依赖哪些知识。现实场景中知识来源多样（上下文、检索、分解、中间推理），形成噪声且冗余的候选空间，而非干净的金标准证据集。现有方法缺乏细粒度的依赖估计能力，且难以处理知识单元间的冗余、替代和互补关系。

Method: 提出Knot，包含三个关键设计：(1) 从子集级别的反事实监督中学习；(2) 通过覆盖潜在依赖因子来建模子集敏感性；(3) 推导排序感知的单元分数以识别有影响力的候选知识单元。

Result: 在多选题和生成式QA基准上，Knot在子集敏感性预测上优于所有基线；在不额外调用QA模型的情况下，生成比可部署基线更忠实的单元排序；用于实际风险筛查时，其依赖分数能帮助早期标记易出错的QA预测。

Conclusion: Knot能有效估计知识依赖关系，在不需要测试时穷举扰动的情况下获得细粒度的依赖分数，并可用于早期风险筛查，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: Reliable question answering requires identifying not only whether an answer is correct, but also which available knowledge the prediction depends on. In realistic LLM-based QA, this knowledge may come from context, retrieval, decomposition, or intermediate reasoning, forming a noisy and redundant candidate space rather than a clean gold evidence set. We study \emph{knowledge dependency estimation}: estimating the sensitivity of a fixed black-box QA model to different candidate knowledge units. The challenge is to obtain fine-grained dependency scores without exhaustive test-time perturbation while modeling redundancy, substitutability, and complementarity. We propose \textbf{Knot}, a structured rank-aware knowledge dependency estimator. Knot learns from subset-level counterfactual supervision, models subset sensitivity through coverage over latent dependency factors, and derives rank-aware unit scores to identify influential candidates. Across multiple-choice and generative QA benchmarks, Knot outperforms all compared baselines in subset-sensitivity prediction and produces more faithful unit rankings than deployable baselines without extra QA-model calls; when used for practical risk screening, its dependency scores help flag error-prone QA predictions early.

### [123] [ConvMemory: A Lightweight Learned Memory Reranker, a Negative Attribution Result, and a Research-Preview Conflict Editor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28062)

We then publish a rigorous negative attribution result on a previously claimed mechanism: a five-seed retrained ablation with paired bootstrap shows that ConvMemory's learned temporal window is statistically significant on aggregate but not temporally specific, with the largest effects on hard non-temporal controls and no significant effect on multi-hop temporal queries. The honest description of the mechanism is cheap cross-encoder distillation in a fused dense+lexical feature space, not temporal-structure exploitation. We additionally release CCGE-LA, a low-amplitude conflict-aware candidate-set editor over ConvMemory, as a research preview with modest but consistent gains on supersession and stale/rescue slices on LoCoMo. All results are retrieval-stage; ConvMemory does not match mxbai-rerank-large-v1 in absolute LoCoMo MRR, and the report is single-author and not yet independently audited.

### [124] [StoryLens: Preference-Aligned Story Rewriting via Context-Aware Narrative Enrichment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28073)
*Hanwen Cui,Yuting Mei,Yuhang Fu,Dingyi Yang,Qin Jin*

TL;DR: 本文提出STORYLENSBENCH基准、STORYLENSEVAL奖励模型和STORYLENSWRITER两阶段改写模型，通过上下文感知的叙事增强实现偏好对齐的故事改写，实验证明该方法显著优于风格迁移等基线。

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [125] [ATLAS: All-round Testing of Long-context Abilities across Scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28079)
*Deli Huang,Cunguang Wang,Hongyin Tang,Zhe Tang,Linsen Guo,Dongyu Ru,Ruoshi Yuan,Ziyue Zhu,Xiaoyu Li,Ziwen Wang,Chen Zhang,Anchun Gui,Wen Zan,Jiaqi Zhang,Xuezhi Cao,Jingang Wang,Xunliang Cai,Yixin Cao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ATLAS是一个重新定义长文本评估的基准框架，提出分层分类法、长度感知AUC评分和ATLAScore指标，揭示模型在8K-1M长度范围内的性能退化曲线，发现排名随长度和任务类别显著变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长文本评测通常报告单一长度或狭窄任务族，掩盖了两种失败模式：性能随长度增长而崩溃、强检索能力不一定迁移到下游任务。需要一种长度相关的能力剖析方法来替代单点指标。

Method: 提出三个方法论原则：(i)分层分类法，将基础操作与应用工作负载分离以归因失败；(ii)长度感知AUC评分，在8K-1M固定网格上积分得分-长度曲线；(iii)ATLAScore，分类别调和平均聚合，并包含端到端不确定性传播。

Result: 在8个能力维度、9个可审计组件、6438个实例上评估26个模型。Gemini-3.1-Pro-Preview在128K领先，Claude-Opus-4.6在1M领先。ATLASscore@8K-128K与@8K-1M之间排名大幅重排：7个模型移动至少2位，两个分类层仅共享61%的交叉模型方差，个别排名差距达12位。

Conclusion: 长文本质量应按能力和长度分别报告，而非单一分数。ATLAS框架为长文本评估提供了更全面、更细粒度的标准。

Abstract: Long-context language models now advertise context windows up to millions of tokens, yet evaluations typically report a single length or a narrow task family, masking two failure modes: performance can collapse as length grows, and strong retrieval need not transfer to downstream use. We present ATLAS, a benchmarking framework that redefines long-context evaluation as length-dependent capability profiling. ATLAS contributes three methodological principles:(i) a layered taxonomy separating foundational operations from application workloads so failures can be attributed, (ii) length-aware AUC scoring that integrates score-length curves over a fixed 8K-1M grid, replacing single-point metrics with full degradation profiles, and (iii) ATLAScore, a harmonic-mean aggregate over taxonomy categories that penalizes imbalanced profiles, with end-to-end uncertainty propagation from subset scores through the nonlinear final aggregate. We instantiate the framework across eight capability dimensions with nine auditable components and 6,438 instances, and evaluate 26 models. Gemini-3.1-Pro-Preview leads at 128K, Claude-Opus-4.6 leads at 1M. Rankings reshuffle substantially between ATLASscore@8K-128K and ATLASscore@8K-1M: 7 models move by at least two ranks, and the two taxonomy layers share only 61% of cross-model variance, with individual rank gaps up to 12 positions. These results support reporting long-context quality by capability and length, not by a single headline score.

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) has emerged as a promising paradigm for enhancing large language models (LLMs) on multi-hop question answering (QA), which requires reasoning over evidence from multiple documents. Current multi-hop RAG methods generally focus on either query-side task decomposition or corpus-side knowledge graph construction. Despite their progress, these methods still struggle to achieve satisfactory performance on complex multi-hop QA tasks. To this end, we propose ConRAG, a consensus-driven multi-view RAG framework that effectively boosts LLMs on complex multi-hop QA. The core of ConRAG is to systematically optimize both the query and corpus sides and to leverage multi-view evidence (relation, entity, and text signals) for more accurate retrieval. Extensive experiments on three multi-hop QA benchmarks show that ConRAG consistently outperforms all baselines by a clear margin, e.g., up to +26.9% average performance gains over vanilla RAG, and enables Gemma-4-31B to achieve a new state-of-the-art record on the challenging MuSiQue benchmark.

### [127] [Ask Now, Use Later: Benchmarking the Proactivity Gap in Long-Lived LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28108)
*Bin Wu,Guanyun Zou,Bingbing Wang,Huan Zhao,Chuan Shi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出并定义了长期LLM智能体中的"主动性问题"——Ask-to-Remember (ATR)，即智能体是否在当前任务中主动询问用户未来可能需要的偏好信息。作者构建了首个ATR基准测试ATRBench，发现当前8个前沿LLM智能体在ATR任务上的表现比已获知偏好信息的oracle低至少62分，且提示工程改进效果有限，诊断表明信息获取是瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期运行的LLM智能体需要跨会话理解用户偏好，但现有智能体只能被动接受用户提供的信息，缺乏主动询问用户未表达但未来可能需要的偏好的能力，导致"主动性差距"（proactivity gap）。随着用户将更多事务委托给智能体，这一差距的影响日益严重。

Method: 本文从主动性差距中隔离出一个具体可控的子问题——Ask-to-Remember (ATR)，并将其形式化为基准测试ATRBench。每个用户的偏好被设为隐藏的ground truth，智能体必须主动询问才能获取，而非依赖记忆或推理。在8个前沿LLM智能体上进行评估，并与已获知相关偏好的oracle进行对比。

Result: 8个前沿LLM智能体的默认表现比oracle低至少62分；通过提示工程改进（prompting）只能缩小很小一部分差距；诊断分析表明信息获取（acquisition）是主要瓶颈环节。

Conclusion: ATRBench揭示了当前LLM智能体在主动性方面的显著不足，并提供了一个可供诊断和测试的基准平台，为后续弥合这一主动性差距的研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: A long-lived LLM agent, such as OpenClaw, earns its value by acting on a user's preferences and constraints across sessions, not just the current request. Yet today's agents keep what a user volunteers but rarely ask for what stays unspoken, leaving a proactivity gap in long-lived LLM agents: an agent cannot act on a preference it never obtained. As users delegate more of their affairs to agents, the impact of this gap grows. We isolate one concrete, controllable slice of this gap as Ask-to-Remember (ATR): the agent decides whether to ask now for a reusable user preference that the current task does not need but a later session with the same user will. ATR is hard even to evaluate: the right question is underdetermined and its payoff deferred to tasks that may never arise. ATRBench, to the best of our knowledge the first ATR benchmark, makes it measurable by fixing each user's preferences as hidden ground truth, so success demands asking, not recall. Across eight frontier LLM agents, defaults fall at least 62 points below an oracle handed the relevant preference, and prompting closes little of it. Diagnostics identify acquisition as the bottleneck. ATRBench surfaces this proactivity gap in current agents and offers a diagnostic testbed for closing it.

</details>

### [128] [Identifying and Understanding Human Values in Text: A Tailorable LLM-based Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27373)
*Eduardo de la Cruz Fernández,Marcelo Karanik,Sascha Ossowski*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的模块化架构，用于从文本中检测和量化人类价值观的强度。该架构包含三个协调模块：从基础理论文本生成结构化价值规范、使用这些规范标注文本、基于修辞和语义证据分配支持或抵抗等级。该架构在ValueEval数据集上进行了评估，展现了良好的检测性能，验证了其通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统效用最大化模型缺乏伦理和道德考量，随着智能系统自主性增强，亟需评估AI决策与人类价值观的一致程度。现有方法受限于特定价值理论或依赖复杂的提示工程，缺乏通用性和可扩展性。

Method: 提出一种三模块LLM架构：(1) 规范生成模块——从任何理论框架的基础文本中生成结构化价值规范；(2) 文本标注模块——使用生成的规范对文本进行标注；(3) 评分模块——基于修辞和语义证据分配等级化的支持或抵抗分数。模块化设计将价值概念化与检测任务分离，保证了可扩展性和可复现性。

Result: 在ValueEval数据集上使用多个LLM进行实例化实验，取得了良好的检测性能，验证了该流水线的通用性。

Conclusion: 该模块化架构成功克服了先前方法对特定价值理论的依赖和复杂的提示工程问题，提供了一种可适应多种理论框架的可扩展、可复现的价值观检测方案。

Abstract: As intelligent systems become more autonomous, the scientific community focuses on creating decision-making mechanisms that include ethical and moral considerations, unlike traditional utility-maximisation models. To achieve this, a key aspect is assessing how well these decisions align with human values. To this end, a promising line of research is centred on developing approaches based on Large Language Models (LLMs) to identify human values from text, whether explicit or implicit, enabling their recognition throughout. This paper introduces a LLM-based architecture to detect and quantify the intensity of human values in text, avoiding the limitations of previous approaches tied to specific value theory or complex prompt engineering. The architecture comprises three coordinated modules: one that generates structured value specifications from the foundational texts of any theoretical framework; one that labels texts using these specifications; and one that assigns graded support or resistance based on rhetorical and semantic evidence. This modular approach separates the tasks of conceptualising from detecting human values, creating a scalable and reproducible process driven by value specifications adaptable to various theories. The architecture was instantiated with multiple LLMs and evaluated using the ValueEval dataset. The experiments demonstrate good detection performance, confirming the generality of the pipeline.

### [129] [On the Origin of Synthetic Information by Means of Steganographic Inheritance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27551)
*Ching-Chun Chang,Isao Echizen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文借鉴生物遗传学中的遗传和进化概念，提出了一种基于隐写术的合成信息溯源机制。该机制通过在合成信息生成时嵌入不可见的亲本特征，使得合成信息在生命周期内均可追溯其来源，从而解决了AI时代合成信息演化过程中难以追溯的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着人工智能生成内容的能力日益强大，合成信息的演化谱系变得越来越难以追踪——一个足够强大的模型生成的"后代"可能在结构和信号层面与父本来源差异巨大，难以辨别其真实来源。这种"溯源危机"对信息真实性、信任机制和人类智力活动产生深远影响，因此亟需一种能够追踪合成信息进化谱系的方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于隐写术的遗传类比机制：(1) 在合成信息（后代）生成时，通过投影器从父本中提取特征（类似遗传性状）；(2) 隐写编码器将该特征不可见地嵌入到后代中，使其在整个生命周期中持续存在；(3) 当需要查询亲本关系时，隐写解码器从后代提取特征，并与参考池中的候选父本特征进行比对，从而确定最可能的亲本。

Result: 理论分析表征了系统发育准确性作为投影器和隐写系统属性的函数关系；跨多种投影器和隐写系统的实验评估证明了所提方法在多种处理操作和语义修改下的可行性。

Conclusion: 设想了一个合成信息生态系统，其中合成信息被赋予隐藏但可追踪的谱系特征，从简单起源不断分支进化，形成无数已存在和正在演化中的信息形态——类比于生物进化中"从简单起源演化出无尽最美丽和最奇异的形态"。

Abstract: The origin of species has been the mystery of mysteries in natural science. By analogy, the origin of synthetic information, we suggest, is the mystery of mysteries in information science. The question carries a moral weight that a technical account can neither fully resolve nor responsibly ignore, as its impact on truth, trust, and human intellect extends deep into the broader economy and society. The very power of artificial intelligence makes the evolutionary lineage of synthetic information grow ever harder to trace, for a sufficiently capable model may generate offspring that bear little resemblance, at either the structural or signal level, to the parent source from which they were derived. As in genetics, two individuals may share the same phenotype mirroring each other in outward appearance, yet differ fundamentally in their genotype. We propose, by means of steganography, a mechanism analogous to heredity. At the moment an offspring is reproduced, a projector derives a trait from the parent, and a steganographic encoder invisibly hides it within the offspring. This trait persists throughout the offspring's life cycle in a cyber ecosystem. When parentage is queried, a steganographic decoder extracts the trait from the offspring and compares it against the traits of candidate parents in a reference pool, thereby nominating the most likely one. A theoretical analysis characterises phylogenetic accuracy as a function of projector and stegosystem properties, whilst empirical evaluations across multiple projectors and stegosystems demonstrate the viability of the proposed methodology under a broad spectrum of processing operations and semantic modifications. We envision a cyber ecosystem in which synthetic information, endowed with hidden yet traceable lineage traits, branches from a simple beginning into endless forms that have been, and are being, evolved.

</details>


### [130] [Why LLMs Fail at Causal Discovery and How Interventional Agents Escape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27567)
*Amartya Roy,Sonali Parbhoo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文证明大语言模型在因果发现任务中存在根本性局限：监督微调、直接偏好优化和上下文学习等方法无法区分产生相似观测数据的因果图，且模型内部表示需无限增长才能做到。作者提出A-CBO方法，将冻结的语言模型作为干预预言机，配合外部贝叶斯循环，在对数轮次内收敛到正确因果图，在Corr2Cause和扩展基准上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明大语言模型在因果发现任务中随着图复杂度增加性能下降，但失败的根本原因尚未明确。本文旨在从理论上证明这一失败是学习范式固有的，而非模型或数据集的特例。

Method: 首先通过核障碍定理形式化证明监督微调、直接偏好优化和上下文学习等方法在因果发现中的根本局限。随后提出Agentic Causal Bayesian Optimization (A-CBO)，将冻结的语言模型作为干预预言机回答关于干预效果的查询，外部贝叶斯循环在对数轮次内集中信念于候选因果图。

Result: 在Corr2Cause上，A-CBO无需训练即可匹配微调基线。在扩展至24变量、18K测试样本的Extended Corr2Cause基准上，A-CBO显著优于微调和偏好优化方法，且优势随问题规模增长而扩大。

Conclusion: 因果发现的局限性是学习范式的固有属性，而非模型缺陷。A-CBO通过将决策空间移出核障碍适用的范围，实现了可证明的收敛性，为利用语言模型进行因果推理提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Causal discovery is a cornerstone of scientific reasoning, yet whether large language models can perform it reliably remains an open question. Recent benchmarks show that even fine-tuned models plateau on simple causal graphs and degrade as complexity grows, but why they fail has not been established. We prove the failure is fundamental: supervised fine-tuning, direct preference optimization, and in-context learning all produce predictors that cannot distinguish between causal graphs generating similar observational data, and any attempt to do so requires the model's internal representations to grow unboundedly, violating the very conditions under which these methods work. We formalize this as a kernel obstruction theorem, establishing that the limitation is intrinsic to the learning paradigm, \emph{not any particular model or dataset}. We propose Agentic Causal Bayesian Optimization (A-CBO), wherein a frozen language model serves as an interventional oracle answering targeted queries about intervention effects, while an external Bayesian loop concentrates beliefs over candidate graphs in logarithmically many rounds. Because the decision operates outside the space where the obstruction applies, A-CBO provably converges while the underlying model remains unchanged. On Corr2Cause, A-CBO matches fine-tuned baselines without any training. On Extended Corr2Cause, a new benchmark scaling to 24 variables with 18K test samples, A-CBO significantly outperforms both fine-tuning and preference optimization, with the advantage growing

</details>


### [131] [RULER: Representation-Level Verification of Machine Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27569)
*Georgina Cosma,Axel Finke*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RULER 提出两种表示级验证指标（M2 和 M4）来检测机器遗忘方法中的残留记忆，发现现有输出级评估无法捕捉表示层的信息残留，且多种遗忘方法在表示层面均存在显著记忆痕迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器遗忘验证仅停留在输出层面（成员推断、保留集准确率、遗忘集准确率），但模型可能在满足所有输出级指标的同时，在中间表示层仍编码了被遗忘记录的信息，因此需要表示层面的验证指标。

Method: 提出 RULER 框架：M2（基于 oracle 的对比指标，衡量遗忘集记录在表示空间中的位置是否与从头重新训练的模型一致）和 M4（无 oracle 指标，仅从遗忘模型内部相似性结构检测残留信号）。使用线性混合效应模型对四种近似遗忘方法和 Bad Teacher 方法进行统计检验。

Result: 四种近似遗忘方法均通过输出级评估，但 M2 在 12 种条件中的 10 种检测到显著残留（p<0.05），且效应量随遗忘比例增大。Bad Teacher 方法表现出相同残留模式。M4 在表格、图像、临床文本和人脸身份多种场景中作为预遗忘诊断工具，检测到人脸识别模型中的身份级记忆未被任何测试方法完全擦除。

Conclusion: 输出级验证不足以评估机器遗忘效果，表示级验证（如 RULER）是必要补充；现有主流遗忘方法在表示层面普遍存在残留记忆，尤其在身份级记忆任务中表现突出。

Abstract: Machine unlearning aims to remove the influence of specific training records from a deployed model without retraining from scratch. Current protocols verify this at the output level through membership inference, retain accuracy, and forget-set accuracy, but a model can satisfy all three whilst still encoding forgotten records in its intermediate representations. We introduce RULER, a set of representation-level verification metrics. The oracle-comparative metric M2 measures whether forget-set records occupy the same representational position as in a model retrained without them. The oracle-free metric M4 detects residuals from the unlearned model's internal similarity structure alone, without retraining. Four approximate unlearning methods all pass output-level evaluation, yet under a linear mixed-effects model M2 detects significant residuals in 10 of 12 conditions (p<0.05), with effect sizes growing as the forget fraction increases. A fifth method, Bad Teacher, shows the same residuals despite a different forgetting mechanism. M4 acts as a pre-unlearning diagnostic across tabular, image, clinical text, and face-identity settings: it detects identity-level memorisation in face recognition models where no tested method fully erases the signal.

</details>


### [132] [LaneRoPE: Positional Encoding for Collaborative Parallel Reasoning and Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27570)
*Gabriele Cesa,Thomas Hehn,Aleix Torres-Camps,Àlex Batlle Casellas,Jordi Ros-Giralt,Arash Behboodi,Tribhuvanesh Orekondy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出LaneRoPE方法，通过在生成时引入序列间注意力掩码和旋转位置编码扩展，实现多个并行序列间的协作，提升数学推理任务准确性，且对模型架构改动极小、推理开销可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的并行LLM测试时扩展技术（如best-of-N）虽能提升准确率并利用批处理效率，但各序列独立生成，无法复用其他序列的中间生成结果、计算或观测信息，导致协作缺失。

Method: 提出LaneRoPE，包含两个关键设计：(a) 序列间注意力掩码，使不同序列的采样相互依赖；(b) 旋转位置编码扩展，注入包含序列内部及跨序列的相对位置信息的编码。

Result: 在数学推理任务上，LaneRoPE实现了序列间的有效协作，在限制生成序列长度的情况下获得了额外的准确率提升。

Conclusion: LaneRoPE以极小的架构改动和可忽略的推理开销实现了并行推理协作，适合快速集成到现有LLM推理流程中。

Abstract: Parallel LLM test-time scaling techniques (e.g., best-of-$N$) require drawing $N>1$ sequences conditioned on the same input prompt. These methods boost accuracy while exploiting the computational efficiency of batching $N$ generations. However, each sequence in the batch is traditionally generated independently and hence does not reuse intermediate generations, computations, or observations from other sequences. In this paper, we propose LaneRoPE to enable coordination and collaboration among $N>1$ sequences at generation time. LaneRoPE involves two key ideas: (a) an inter-sequence attention mask to make sampling of sequences dependent on one another; and (b) a RoPE extension that injects positional information that captures relative positions between tokens, both within and outside a particular sequence. We evaluate our approach on mathematical reasoning tasks and find promising results: LaneRoPE enables collaboration among sequences, yielding additional accuracy gains under limited generated sequence length. Importantly, since LaneRoPE enables coordination with minimal changes to the underlying LLM architecture and introduces a negligible overhead at inference time, it is appealing to rapidly incorporate parallel reasoning into existing LLM inference pipelines.

### [135] [You Are in Control of Your State: Why Human Outcomes Are Controllable Through Causal State Intervention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27580)
*Suraj Biswas,Saurav Gupta,Pritam Mukherjee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出人类行为变异性的根源在于动态潜在状态（即时间索引的权重向量），该状态因果性地决定决策与结果，并通过干预状态轨迹实现对人类结果的条件性控制。基于六条证据链和超过20万用户的24个月观测数据，推导出七个可检验预测和六项操作要求，应用于数字健康、教育、AI个性化等领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 行为科学和面向人类的人工智能面临一个核心谜题：个体内变异性的持续存在——相同个体面对相同输入却产生不同输出，且个体间的差异无法被可观测协变量完全解释。本文旨在论证这种变异性应归因于个体的动态潜在状态，并证明通过针对状态及其在决策形成时刻的权重进行干预，可以在精确和可操作的意义上控制人类结果。

Method: 本文首先定义了状态的概念：一个时间索引的权重向量，涵盖个体生物学、生理学和神经心理学处理下一个事件为决策和结果的维度。论证了状态与决策、结果之间是因果关系而非相关关系，且权重向量在亚日时间尺度上动态变化，意识通道是依赖于状态的窄注意瓶颈。通过六条已有证据（因果推断、预测加工、稳态应变、注意瓶颈、时间生物学、计算精神病学）和来自部署行为平台的24个月观测数据（2023-2026年，涵盖20万以上用户、四种职业角色）来验证框架。

Result: 推导出七个可检验的预测，列出了状态感知系统的六项操作要求，并讨论了该框架对数字健康、教育、AI个性化和个人能动性的启示。

Conclusion: 本文的核心主张是：给定事件的结果在条件上可控于干预时刻的状态轨迹。这意味着通过理解并干预个体的动态状态权重向量，可以实现对人类行为更精确的预测和控制，为行为科学和人机交互提供新的理论框架和实践指导。

Abstract: A central puzzle for the behavioural sciences and for human-facing artificial intelligence is the persistence of within-person variability. The same individual, presented with the same observable input, produces different outcomes on different occasions, and different individuals produce divergent outcomes that no observable covariate fully predicts. We argue that this variability belongs in the dynamic latent state of the person, and that human outcomes are controllable in a precise and operational sense through interventions that target the state and its weighting at the moment a decision is being formed.
  We define a state as the time-indexed weighting vector over the dimensions that govern how an individual's biology, physiology, and neuropsychology process the next event into a decision and an outcome. The relationship between state, decision, and outcome is causal rather than correlational. The weighting vector is dynamic at sub-daily timescales. The conscious channel through which outcomes are reportable is a narrow attentional bottleneck whose contents are themselves state-dependent. Taken together, these claims imply that the outcome of a given event is controllable, conditionally, on the state-trajectory at the time of intervention.
  We motivate the framework with six strands of established evidence (causal inference, predictive processing, allostasis, attentional bottleneck, chronobiology, computational psychiatry) and a 24-month observational base from a deployed behavioural platform spanning more than 200,000 consented users across four occupational personas (research period 2023 to 2026). We derive seven testable predictions, list six operational requirements for state-aware systems, and discuss implications for digital health, education, AI personalisation, and personal agency.

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 即使是明确标注为不公平和有害的共谋工具，安全对齐的LLM智能体在能获得战略优势时仍会自愿接受并采用。研究在Liar's Bar和Cleanup两个多智能体环境中测试了12个模型和6种提示变体，发现大多数智能体明知工具不公平却仍接受，且仅靠公平性标签或基础对齐无法可靠阻止共谋，只有明确的伦理框架才能减少采纳，但对小模型效果有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建两个战略性多智能体环境（Liar's Bar竞争性欺骗场景和Cleanup混合动机资源管理场景），向智能体提供能带来显著优势但明确损害其他智能体的秘密共谋工具。在12个模型（7B、70B及闭源规模）和6种提示变体上进行系统测试。

Conclusion: 首次系统性地研究了LLM多智能体系统中自愿共谋采纳行为，表明防止此类行为需要明确的安全防护机制，而非依赖通用对齐。

Abstract: Even when a tool is explicitly described as unfair and harmful to others, ostensibly safety-aligned LLM agents still voluntarily engage in secret collusion whenever doing so confers a strategic advantage. To investigate this phenomenon, we introduce an empirical framework built on two strategic multi-agent environments: Liar's Bar, a competitive deception scenario, and Cleanup, a mixed-motive resource-management scenario, in which agents are offered secret collusion tools that provide significant advantages while clearly disadvantaging the other agents. Across 12 models (at the 7B, 70B, and proprietary scales) and 6 prompt variants, we find that most agents consistently accept these tools and develop collusive strategies, while explicitly acknowledging the unfairness of the tools before accepting. We further show that neither the unfairness labels nor baseline alignment alone reliably deters collusion: only explicit ethical framing reduces adoption and, even then, smaller models remain susceptible. More broadly, our work presents the first systematic investigation of voluntary collusion adoption in LLM-based multi-agent systems, and suggests that preventing such behaviour requires explicit safeguards rather than reliance on general alignment.

Abstract: Alignment faking (AF) refers to a model strategically complying with a training objective to avoid behavioural modification while preserving its deployment preferences. Understanding when and why AF arises matters as models grow better at distinguishing training from deployment. Prior work finds AF fragile, prompt-sensitive, and model-dependent, leaving its underlying drivers unclear. We study AF in a controlled, minimal setup that isolates its core components, and observe it across a wider range of models than previously reported, including small-scale models. We identify three separable drivers -- values, goal guarding, and sycophancy -- and show via targeted prompt ablations and activation steering that each independently modulates AF behaviour. Our results indicate AF is more widespread than previously reported and that its occurrence is predictable from situational cues and measurable model tendencies such as baseline sycophancy and stated values. ### [139] [Cross-Entropy Games and Frost Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27701)
*Arthur Renard,Franck Gabriel,Valentin Hartmann,Clément Hongler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Frost Training是一种利用奖励函数在嵌入空间中的梯度来改进基于蒙特卡洛的策略优化方法，专门用于处理称为交叉熵游戏的LLM-as-a-judge任务。该方法借鉴了GCG越狱技术中的梯度信号，首次将其应用于模型训练增强，通过GRPO训练进行最大似然填充验证。实验表明，该方法能提升模型生成高得分输出的能力，在best-of-k设置中达到更高最大分数，且训练速度更快。

Method: 利用奖励函数在嵌入空间中的梯度信号（即GCG越狱技术中使用的梯度）来辅助模型训练，结合GRPO训练进行最大似然填充。

Result: 在best-of-k设置中达到更高最大分数，且训练速度更快。

Conclusion: Frost Training能够有效提升基于蒙特卡洛的策略优化性能，将原本用于越狱的梯度信号成功转化为训练增强信号。

Abstract: We present Frost Training, a method for improving Monte Carlo-based policy optimization for a large family of LLM-as-a-judge tasks called Cross-Entropy Games. The key idea is to exploit the gradient of the reward function in embedding space. This signal is used in the Greedy Coordinate Gradient (GCG) jailbreaking technique; we demonstrate for the first time that it can also be used to boost model training. We validate our method using GRPO training for maximum-likelihood infilling. Frost Training improves the model's ability to generate high-scoring outputs, reaching higher maximum scores in a best-of-k setting, and does so at an increased speed.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在智能体系统中需遵循结构化协议并适应动态状态，但提示扩展在紧凑模型上易超出有效提示域，而部署时微调受限于数据与计算资源稀缺。

Method: 采用分层控制-学习框架：先蒸馏使紧凑模型学习输出模式，再由Oracle-Controller循环在线监督——控制器监控协议有效性与语义性能，将历史投影到可行提示域，在漂移时触发轻量级Oracle监督微调。

Result: 在多保真贝叶斯优化测试中，所提方法在可靠性和成本效率上优于非分层、仅蒸馏及非蒸馏基线。

Conclusion: 分离模式学习与语义适应是提升智能体系统中LLM部署可靠性与成本效率的有效策略。

Abstract: Large Language Models are increasingly deployed inside agentic systems, where they must follow structured protocols, adapt to evolving states, and operate under memory, latency, and cost constraints. In such regimes, prompt extension is unreliable: growing contexts can push compact models outside their effective prompt domain, while deployment-time fine-tuning remains limited by scarce data and compute. We propose a hierarchical control-and-learning framework in which a compact model is first distilled to learn the required output schema, then supervised online by an oracle-controller loop. The controller monitors protocol validity and semantic performance, projects accumulated histories into a feasible prompt domain, and triggers lightweight oracle-supervised fine-tuning under drift. This separates schema learning for communication compatibility from semantic adaptation for task-level correction. We formalize prompt-domain feasibility and attention-induced saturation, motivating control of the effective prompt state rather than reliance on nominal context length. Using Multi-Fidelity Bayesian Optimization as a controlled sequential testbed, we characterize a core deployment failure mode and show improved reliability and cost-efficiency over non-hierarchical, distillation-only, and non-distilled baselines.
